The app bar holds a navigation list of all currently open pages in the app bar.\r\n\r\nThe user can enable / disable some app bar animation when a new page is added via the app's settings.\r\n\r\nAnother configuration setting is available to set the way the navigation list reacts on user interaction. One option is to open an existing tab by just tapping on it (single tap). To select an item from the navigation list, the user has to right tap it. The app gives visual feedback when right tapping is registered.\r\n\r\nThe other option is to select the navigation item by a single tap and open the page by double tapping.
